class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_fixed_size_thread_pool}{Fixed\+Size\+Thread\+Pool}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A thread pool where works are accessed concurrently by blocking other threads. A thread pool that contains fixed number of threads for work processing. It is a blocking pool, i.\+e., works are enqueued and dequeued concurrently by blocking other threads, in FIFO order. The pool can be used concurrently, namely, it is thread-\/safe. However, the user must ensure that the pool is properly initialized before subsequent usages. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_masked_intersectable}{Masked\+Intersectable}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Carve out some part of an intersectable. This is a masking approach based on intersection routine. Another common approach to shape masking is BSDF-\/based, where the mask determines whether the incoming light simply passes through (a no-\/op, perfectly transmitting BSDF). There is a trade-\/off between these approaches\+: masking in intersection routine samples the mask texture (usually a slower operation) in the tight loop of acceleration structure traversal, while masking in BSDF will need to re-\/enter the acceleration structure multiple times (such as when rendering a forest) which can also be slow. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_array_heap}{TArray\+Heap}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A fixed size heap backed by an array. The container inherits the properties of a fixed size array of type {\ttfamily T}. The container keeps all {\ttfamily N} elements alive until its lifetime ends, even if elements are popped/removed from the stack. It is guaranteed that no dynamic memory allocation takes place. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_array_stack}{TArray\+Stack}}

The container keeps all {\ttfamily N} elements alive until its lifetime ends, even if elements are popped/removed from the stack. It is guaranteed that no dynamic memory allocation takes place. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_array_vector}{TArray\+Vector}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A fixed size vector backed by an array. The container inherits the properties of a fixed size array of type {\ttfamily T}. The container keeps all {\ttfamily N} elements alive until its lifetime ends, even if elements are popped/removed from the vector. It is guaranteed that no dynamic memory allocation takes place. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_atomic_quasi_queue}{TAtomic\+Quasi\+Queue}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A multi-\/producer, multi-\/consumer, lock-\/free concurrent queue-\/like structure. For single-\/thread uses, it is a FIFO queue. For multi-\/thread uses, it is {\itshape mostly} a FIFO queue. Specifically, items put in by a given producer will all come out in the same order (FIFO). But there is no coordination between items from other producers--two items put in by two different producers will come out in an undefined order relative to each other (the interleaving between different streams of items from different producers is undefined, even with external synchronization). It is possible some items will starve in the queue if more items are enqueued than dequeued. Guarantees aquire-\/release semantics for items that are enqueued/dequeued. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_bilinear_pixel_tex2_d}{TBilinear\+Pixel\+Tex2D}}
\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_binary_bvh_intersector}{TBinary\+Bvh\+Intersector}}

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_blockable_atomic_quasi_queue}{TBlockable\+Atomic\+Quasi\+Queue}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Blockable version of the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_t_atomic_quasi_queue}{TAtomic\+Quasi\+Queue}}. For single-\/thread uses, it is a FIFO queue. For multi-\/thread uses, it is {\itshape mostly} a FIFO queue. Specifically, items put in by a given producer will all come out in the same order (FIFO). But there is no coordination between items from other producers--two items put in by two different producers will come out in an undefined order relative to each other (the interleaving between different streams of items from different producers is undefined, even with external synchronization). It is possible some items will starve in the queue if more items are enqueued than dequeued. Guarantees aquire-\/release semantics for items that are enqueued/dequeued. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Texture storing one single constant of arbitrary type. This texture provides only a constant value. Input color usages are ignored. class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_sdl_resource_base}{TSdl\+Resource\+Base}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A convenient \doxylink{classph_1_1_i_sdl_resource}{ISdl\+Resource} with core requirements implemented. This class is similar to \doxylink{classph_1_1_sdl_resource_base}{Sdl\+Resource\+Base}, except that it provides a way for derived classes to supply static category information. Dynamic category is directly obtained from it. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_sdl_resource_identifier}{TSdl\+Resource\+Identifier}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A field class that binds a resource identifier member. Though the member type that is binded by default can handle any types of identifier (the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_resource_identifier}{Resource\+Identifier}} class, which represents a PRI), this class treat it as a SDL Resource Identifier (SRI) which has a more specific form. On some circumstances it may be desirable to accept any identifier, and this can be achieved by specifying {\ttfamily IS\+\_\+\+SRI=false}. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_s_p_s_c_executor}{TSPSCExecutor}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em A single-\/producer, single-\/consumer worker thread. Ctor and dtor are not thread safe. Most of the methods are either producer thread only, or thread-\/safe. {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_t_s_p_s_c_executor_a0d4416821710b9c3c01b9798376a9f4e}{start()}} must be called before adding work since it also serves as a mean to determine the producer thread. Setters for function callbacks can only be called before {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_t_s_p_s_c_executor_a0d4416821710b9c3c01b9798376a9f4e}{start()}}. Note that if work processor is not set from ctor, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_t_s_p_s_c_executor_aff408fe833f82bb136083d0e62ff8592}{set\+Work\+Processor()}} must be called with a valid processor function. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_s_p_s_c_ring_buffer}{TSPSCRing\+Buffer}}

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_swizzled_texture}{TSwizzled\+Texture}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Swizzle an array-\/like input type to the other array-\/like output type. Output type {\ttfamily OutputT} can have any number of elements (no need to be the same as input type {\ttfamily InputT}). For any elements in {\ttfamily OutputT} that is not part of the swizzle, the value will be as if the element is zero-\/initialized (or default-\/initialized depending on the actual type). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

{\footnotesize template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ }\\\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a7bddcd600f81212f4e8ff4071dc640b7}{estimate\+\_\+certainly\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy}} (const std\+::size\+\_\+t view\+Path\+Length, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&X, const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&view\+Path\+Throughput, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&photon\+Map\+Info, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}scene, const std\+::size\+\_\+t min\+Full\+Path\+Length=1, const std\+::size\+\_\+t max\+Full\+Path\+Length=\mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Estimate the energy that can never be obtained by utilizing a photon map. The estimation is for the current hit point only. To account for lost energy along a path with multiple hit points, call this function for each hit point and sum the results. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
{\footnotesize template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ }\\\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending}} (const std\+::size\+\_\+t view\+Path\+Length, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&X, const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&view\+Path\+Throughput, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&photon\+Map\+Info, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}scene, const std\+::size\+\_\+t min\+Full\+Path\+Length=1, const std\+::size\+\_\+t max\+Full\+Path\+Length=\mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Estimate the energy that is otherwise lost forever if the path is extended. The estimation is for the current hit point only. To account for lost energy along an extended path with multiple hit points, call this function for each hit point and sum the results. For a hit point, only one of {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a45199b25a540099512e7209137092fdf}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging()}} can be called. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
{\footnotesize template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ }\\\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a45199b25a540099512e7209137092fdf}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging}} (const std\+::size\+\_\+t view\+Path\+Length, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&X, const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&view\+Path\+Throughput, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&photon\+Map\+Info, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}scene, const std\+::size\+\_\+t min\+Full\+Path\+Length=1, const std\+::size\+\_\+t max\+Full\+Path\+Length=\mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Estimate the energy that is otherwise lost forever if the path is merged. The estimation is for the current hit point only and is expected to be called when the path ended (merged). For a hit point, only one of {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a45199b25a540099512e7209137092fdf}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging()}} can be called. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\item

\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
{\footnotesize template$<$typename T $>$ }\\T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a88bc0d52718506077c4752738e833235}{ptr\+\_\+access}} (T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const ptr)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Access a target\textquotesingle{}s member consistently using {\ttfamily .} or {\ttfamily -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} operators. Note that these functions treat smart pointers as regular objects ({\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a88bc0d52718506077c4752738e833235}{ptr\+\_\+access()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a23d56151345e21e253f6d2894ea08a7f}{ref\+\_\+access()}} will refer to the object itself, not its managed data). A nice discussion for the topic\+: \href{https://stackoverflow.com/questions/14466620/c-template-specialization-calling-methods-on-types-that-could-be-pointers-or}{\texttt{ https\+://stackoverflow.\+com/questions/14466620/c-\/template-\/specialization-\/calling-\/methods-\/on-\/types-\/that-\/could-\/be-\/pointers-\/or}}. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
{\footnotesize template$<$typename T $>$ }\\T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a1331f56249b565cedee1ca5996f725a8}{ptr\+\_\+access}} (T \&ref)
\item 
{\footnotesize template$<$typename T $>$ }\\T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a3f8d3b88dfcd683429e5b7746e2b7870}{ptr\+\_\+access}} (T \&\&ref)=delete
\item

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TSpan}{TSpan}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a5390437e1d7fd7d167c847677ea146e6} 
template$<$typename T , std\+::size\+\_\+t EXTENT = std\+::dynamic\+\_\+extent$>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a5390437e1d7fd7d167c847677ea146e6}{ph\+::\+TSpan}} = std\+::span$<$T, EXTENT$>$}



A contiguous sequence of objects of type {\ttfamily T}. Effectively the same as {\ttfamily std\+::span}. 

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a06c532bb78132f63638ec3ef52d46ff3}\index{ph@{ph}!TSpanView@{TSpanView}}
\index{TSpanView@{TSpanView}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TSpanView}{TSpanView}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a06c532bb78132f63638ec3ef52d46ff3} 
template$<$typename T , std\+::size\+\_\+t EXTENT = std\+::dynamic\+\_\+extent$>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a06c532bb78132f63638ec3ef52d46ff3}{ph\+::\+TSpan\+View}} = std\+::span$<$const T, EXTENT$>$}



Same as {\ttfamily TSpan}, except that the objects are const-\/qualified. Note that for pointer types, the const is applied on the pointer itself. For example, when {\ttfamily T} is {\ttfamily const int\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}, the accessed type will be {\ttfamily const int\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} const}.

\index{EEmitterFeatureSet@{EEmitterFeatureSet}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EEmitterFeatureSet}{EEmitterFeatureSet}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a16b931b405833c11fca5c86a7514e603} 
enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a16b931b405833c11fca5c86a7514e603}{ph\+::\+EEmitter\+Feature\+Set}} \+: \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1detail_a28be57d5ff0fc9e06d3980ebb8e7409f}{detail\+::\+Emitter\+Flag\+Int\+Type}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Runtime features of an emitter. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
Some features are not handled by {\ttfamily \doxylink{classph_1_1_emitter}{Emitter}} itself, as it is impossible to determine the intended usage solely from its interface. Currently, light transport algorithms need to handle {\ttfamily Zero\+Bounce\+Sample} and {\ttfamily Bsdf\+Sample} by themselves. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f}\index{ph@{ph}!EMaskingShadowing@{EMaskingShadowing}}
\index{EMaskingShadowing@{EMaskingShadowing}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EMaskingShadowing}{EMaskingShadowing}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f} 
enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f}{ph\+::\+EMasking\+Shadowing}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Different types of masking and shadowing terms for microfacet distributions. Eric Heitz has published a detailed explanation \cite{Heitz:2014:Microfacet}, which is excellent and definitely worth a read in my opinion. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{HightCorrelated@{HightCorrelated}!ph@{ph}}\index{ph@{ph}!HightCorrelated@{HightCorrelated}}}\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095faa87be3fbbfdee88228800d38d3c9246f}\label{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f} 
Hight\+Correlated&Modeling the correlation between masking and shadowing due to the height of the microsurface. This is a more accurate version than the one used by Walter et al. \cite{Walter:2007:Microfacet} (which is {\ttfamily Separable}). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Separable@{Separable}!ph@{ph}}\index{ph@{ph}!Separable@{Separable}}}\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095fa218140cc94a645f77dd15a2af6f640c2}\label{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f} 
Separable&Statistically independent masking and shadowing. This form is simpelr but always overestimates the geometry term as some correlation always exists. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{DirectionCorrelated@{DirectionCorrelated}!ph@{ph}}\index{ph@{ph}!DirectionCorrelated@{DirectionCorrelated}}}\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095fa825264b26cbc9ca8644b00dd60a302b7}\label{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f} 
Direction\+Correlated&Modeling the correlation between masking and shadowing due to the differences between incident and outgoing directions. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{HeightDirectionCorrelated@{HeightDirectionCorrelated}!ph@{ph}}\index{ph@{ph}!HeightDirectionCorrelated@{HeightDirectionCorrelated}}}\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095fa64b4251e86241ad733ecea97639e9492}\label{namespaceph_a0c0fa392ffb753722f245acbe724095f} 
Height\+Direction\+Correlated&Modeling the correlation between masking and shadowing due to both height and direction differences. This is the most accurate version of all. \\

Status of a rendering region. Note that when adding new entries, the order is important\+: later entries will take precedence when multiple regions are merged together. For example, merging {\ttfamily Invalid} and {\ttfamily Updating} regions will result in an {\ttfamily Updating} region.

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a7bddcd600f81212f4e8ff4071dc640b7}\index{ph@{ph}!estimate\_certainly\_lost\_energy@{estimate\_certainly\_lost\_energy}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{estimate\_certainly\_lost\_energy()}{estimate\_certainly\_lost\_energy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a7bddcd600f81212f4e8ff4071dc640b7} 
template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} ph\+::estimate\+\_\+certainly\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{view\+Path\+Length}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&}]{X}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&}]{view\+Path\+Throughput}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&}]{photon\+Map\+Info}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{scene}{, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{min\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{max\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Estimate the energy that can never be obtained by utilizing a photon map. The estimation is for the current hit point only. To account for lost energy along a path with multiple hit points, call this function for each hit point and sum the results. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em view\+Path\+Length} & Current view path length. Each path length calculates an independent component of the total energy (in equilibrium). \\
\hline
{\em X} & Current hit point. \\
\hline
{\em view\+Path\+Throughput} & Current view path throughput. \\
\hline
{\em photon\+Map\+Info} & Information of the photon map that is being involved in the energy evaluation process. \\
\hline
{\em scene} & The scene that is being rendered. \\
\hline
{\em min\+Full\+Path\+Length} & The minimum length of the full light transport path to consider. \\
\hline
{\em max\+Full\+Path\+Length} & The maximum length of the full light transport path to consider (inclusive). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The energy that is lost, properly weighted by {\ttfamily view\+Path\+Throughput}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}\index{ph@{ph}!estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending@{estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending}}
\index{estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending@{estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending()}{estimate\_lost\_energy\_for\_extending()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8} 
template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} ph\+::estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{view\+Path\+Length}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&}]{X}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&}]{view\+Path\+Throughput}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&}]{photon\+Map\+Info}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{scene}{, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{min\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{max\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Estimate the energy that is otherwise lost forever if the path is extended. The estimation is for the current hit point only. To account for lost energy along an extended path with multiple hit points, call this function for each hit point and sum the results. For a hit point, only one of {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a45199b25a540099512e7209137092fdf}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging()}} can be called. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em view\+Path\+Length} & Current view path length. Each path length calculates an independent component of the total energy (in equilibrium). \\
\hline
{\em X} & Current hit point. \\
\hline
{\em view\+Path\+Throughput} & Current view path throughput. \\
\hline
{\em photon\+Map\+Info} & Information of the photon map that is being involved in the energy evaluation process. \\
\hline
{\em scene} & The scene that is being rendered. \\
\hline
{\em min\+Full\+Path\+Length} & The minimum length of the full light transport path to consider. \\
\hline
{\em max\+Full\+Path\+Length} & The maximum length of the full light transport path to consider (inclusive). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The energy that is lost, properly weighted by {\ttfamily view\+Path\+Throughput}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

template$<$CPhoton Photon$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} ph\+::estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{view\+Path\+Length}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_surface_hit}{Surface\+Hit}} \&}]{X}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceph_1_1math_ad1ddf3801f5a9ea201227d49747987ed}{math\+::\+Spectrum}} \&}]{view\+Path\+Throughput}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_t_photon_map_info}{TPhoton\+Map\+Info}}$<$ Photon $>$ \&}]{photon\+Map\+Info}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_scene}{Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{scene}{, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{min\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{max\+Full\+Path\+Length}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_p_m_common_params_add7ec0cd3fbcd49279d13ef7a77f4b57}{PMCommon\+Params\+::\+DEFAULT\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+LENGTH}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Estimate the energy that is otherwise lost forever if the path is merged. The estimation is for the current hit point only and is expected to be called when the path ended (merged). For a hit point, only one of {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a4157e74ef0b3f83ee81fb342f3cdb0b8}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+extending()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a45199b25a540099512e7209137092fdf}{estimate\+\_\+lost\+\_\+energy\+\_\+for\+\_\+merging()}} can be called.

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a60da5e7ab42a0d3a36a7f295bc195104}\index{ph@{ph}!init\_render\_engine@{init\_render\_engine}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{init\_render\_engine()}{init\_render\_engine()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a60da5e7ab42a0d3a36a7f295bc195104} 
bool ph\+::init\+\_\+render\+\_\+engine (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::optional$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_engine_init_settings}{Engine\+Init\+Settings}} $>$}]{settings}{ = {\ttfamily std\+:\+:nullopt}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize the render engine. 

Must be called before any other use of the engine. This functions also initializes all dependencies. Note that initialization is generally not required when using APIs from a base library (e.\+g., the {\ttfamily Common} library)--in case of an exception (such as logging), consult the API\textquotesingle{}s documentation to see if anything should be done before using it.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em settings} & Settings for the engine. If not provided, the engine will try to load from a standard location (automatically create a default one if not exist). \\

\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a4bb82cb7d948a7f9feca7dffb744e02f}\index{ph@{ph}!parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}}
\index{parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parallel\_work()}{parallel\_work()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a4bb82cb7d948a7f9feca7dffb744e02f} 
void ph\+::parallel\+\_\+work (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{num\+Workers}{, }\item[{std\+::function$<$ void(std\+::size\+\_\+t worker\+Idx) $>$}]{work}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Runs specified works in parallel. The function will block the calling thread until all works are complete. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em num\+Workers} & Number of workers running the works. \\
\hline
{\em work} & The actual work that is going to be executed; where the index of the executing worker is specified as input. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{namespaceph_af97a91c8284655b7b30f7e815137585a}\index{ph@{ph}!parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}}
\index{parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parallel\_work()}{parallel\_work()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_af97a91c8284655b7b30f7e815137585a} 
void ph\+::parallel\+\_\+work (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{total\+Work\+Size}{, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{num\+Workers}{, }\item[{std\+::function$<$ void(std\+::size\+\_\+t worker\+Idx, std\+::size\+\_\+t work\+Begin, std\+::size\+\_\+t work\+End) $>$}]{work}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Runs specified works in parallel. The function will block the calling thread until all works are complete. Note that 0-\/sized works are not executed ({\ttfamily work} is not called in this case). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em total\+Work\+Size} & Total amount of work. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Workers} & Number of workers running the works. \\
\hline
{\em work} & The actual work that is going to be executed; where the index range {\ttfamily \mbox{[}work\+Begin, work\+End)} is specified as input, as well as the index of the executing worker. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{namespaceph_ae17e9e02b729060f7221d4fe9b9636b2}\index{ph@{ph}!parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}}
\index{parallel\_work@{parallel\_work}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parallel\_work()}{parallel\_work()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_ae17e9e02b729060f7221d4fe9b9636b2} 
void ph\+::parallel\+\_\+work (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classph_1_1_fixed_size_thread_pool}{Fixed\+Size\+Thread\+Pool}} \&}]{workers}{, }\item[{const std\+::size\+\_\+t}]{total\+Work\+Size}{, }\item[{std\+::function$<$ void(std\+::size\+\_\+t worker\+Idx, std\+::size\+\_\+t work\+Begin, std\+::size\+\_\+t work\+End) $>$}]{work}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Runs specified works in parallel using a thread pool. The function will block the calling thread until all works are complete. Note that 0-\/sized works are not executed ({\ttfamily work} is not called in this case). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em workers} & The thread pool to use. \\
\hline
{\em total\+Work\+Size} & Total amount of work. \\
\hline
{\em work} & The actual work that is going to be executed; where the index range {\ttfamily \mbox{[}work\+Begin, work\+End)} is specified as input, as well as the index of the executing worker. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a3f8d3b88dfcd683429e5b7746e2b7870} 
template$<$typename T $>$ \\
T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ph\+::ptr\+\_\+access (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T \&\&}]{ref}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [delete]}}

All remaining types are forbidden. This forwarding reference overload also prevent the use of rvalue to guard against potential dangling pointer. \Hypertarget{namespaceph_a1331f56249b565cedee1ca5996f725a8}\index{ph@{ph}!ptr\_access@{ptr\_access}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a1331f56249b565cedee1ca5996f725a8} 
template$<$typename T $>$ \\
T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ph\+::ptr\+\_\+access (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T \&}]{ref}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\Hypertarget{namespaceph_a88bc0d52718506077c4752738e833235}\index{ph@{ph}!ptr\_access@{ptr\_access}}
\index{ptr\_access@{ptr\_access}!ph@{ph}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ptr\_access()}{ptr\_access()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceph_a88bc0d52718506077c4752738e833235} 
template$<$typename T $>$ \\
T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ph\+::ptr\+\_\+access (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const}]{ptr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Access a target\textquotesingle{}s member consistently using {\ttfamily .} or {\ttfamily -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} operators. Note that these functions treat smart pointers as regular objects ({\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a88bc0d52718506077c4752738e833235}{ptr\+\_\+access()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespaceph_a23d56151345e21e253f6d2894ea08a7f}{ref\+\_\+access()}} will refer to the object itself, not its managed data). A nice discussion for the topic\+: \href{https://stackoverflow.com/questions/14466620/c-template-specialization-calling-methods-on-types-that-could-be-pointers-or}{\texttt{ https\+://stackoverflow.\+com/questions/14466620/c-\/template-\/specialization-\/calling-\/methods-\/on-\/types-\/that-\/could-\/be-\/pointers-\/or}}.
